<Review>Chris Sung was our Service Advisor for my first visit at Audi San Francisco.  The service website makes it easy to book a service appointment. Appreciated the coverage of Uber to and from our city residence to the center.  Chris was efficient and quick to look into my questions and repairs.  Due to city ordinances the service center is not able to offer car wash, but they did a terrific job of keeping the car clean and safe in times of COVID19.  My only dissatisfaction is the size of the service center.  Being in a dense urban area poses a challenge of course.  I tend to enjoy larger facilities to truly have an enjoyable service experience. Working remote we tend to look forward to errands that keep us out of our normal routines these days, would be nice to be able to enjoy a large facility.  Overall I highly recommend this service center for any AUDI owner in the city/downtown area of San Francisco.</Review>< userid>

I told him what was wrong with the vehicle, as I had it diagnosed at another Audi service center in SAC.   He stated I had to pay $225 for a new diagnostic service, and another estimated $825.00 for the repair.    Since Chris is totally "clueless," he didn't take time to know my car was a TDI and was under the current Audi warranty program,....which has a "full warranty" on the automobile!  Chris refunded my $225, but did so reluctantly and with a very cocky disposition, and also said he did everything correctly.   He was so unprofessional, and completely mis-represented his company. <Pictures>None</Pictures>< Text>
After a horrific incident at a different agency, I was desperate to switch to a more reliable Farmers Insurance office. I called the office a while back, and Alexis, a super friendly auto agent, helped me do the most effortless transition. Alexis walked me through all the steps, made sure I could save more on discounts, and provided exceptional customer service! Susie, the life agent, was terrific and extremely patient! I had acquired life insurance quotes for the family, and she made the whole process a piece of cake! She was very knowledgeable about what she was doing and answered all of our questions in areas we were confused. Rene, the customer service representative, left me in shock. I had never experienced this best top-notch guest service at an insurance office before. I called in asking a couple questions, and he told me to rest assured he would call me the next morning for an update. That very next morning, he was ready with all the answers I asked for and even walked me through filling out some paperwork Farmers requested. He did not end that phone call until he made sure I was satisfied with the service provided. Alexis, Wendy, and Rene went above and beyond, ensuring I was happy and feeling I was in good hands. This office truly values its customers, and would no doubt recommend this agency to friends! Thank you for all you do! Alex get these staff a raise, they earned it !<//Text>
